<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: 30px; text-indent: -0.5in; text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino; color: #ffffff; background-color: #808080;"><b><span style="line-height: 115%;">Spiritual Message for the Day  Karma Yoga by Sri Swami Sivananada</span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: 30px; text-indent: -0.5in; text-align: center;"><strong style="text-indent: -0.5in;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest | 18 May 2015 17.42 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span></strong></p>
<hr />
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Karma Yoga<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Divine Life Society Publication: </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/amrita.htm#_VPID_3"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Amrita Gita</b></span></a></span><b> by Sri Swami Sivananda<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<ol style="margin-top: 0in;" start="1" type="1">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Work is worship of the Lord. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Karma Yoga is the Yoga of selfless action, without agency and expectation of fruits. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Karma Yoga removes the impurities of the mind. It is a potent purifier of the heart. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Karma Yoga prepares the mind for the reception of Divine Light, Divine Grace, and Divine Knowledge. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">See God in every face. Behold the Lord in all creatures. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Share what you have with others. Serve the saints and sages. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Serve the sick. Serve the poor. Serve your parents. Serve your motherland. Serve humanity in general. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Scrutinise always your inner motives. Destroy selfish motives. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Work without egoism. Cultivate the Nimitta-Bhava. Feel you are an instrument in the hands of the Lord. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Surrender always your actions and their fruits to the Lord. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Have equal vision and balanced mind in pleasure and pain, gain and loss, success and failure. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Develop nicely adaptability. Serve always with Atma-Bhava and Narayana-Bhava. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Sing Sitaram, Radheshyam or Hare Rama while you work. Remember the Lord always. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Give up Abhimana of all sorts. Kill the Vairagya-abhimana, Seva-abhimana, Tyagi-abhimana, Kartritva-abhimana, male-female-abhimana, and doctor-judge-abhimana. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Do not expect even thanks or appreciation for your work. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Do actions as your duty, duty for dutys sake. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Never say: I have helped that man. Feel and think: That man gave me an opportunity to serve. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Watch for opportunities for service. Never miss even a single opportunity. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Cultivate amiable, loving, social nature, generosity, catholic nature. Kill selfishness. Control the senses, practise self-restraint, tolerance, sympathy and mercy. These are the qualifications of a Karma Yogi. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Bear insult, injury, harsh words, criticism, heat and cold. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">If you are a doctor, treat the poor free of charge. If you are an advocate, plead for the poor. If you are a teacher or a professor, give free tuition to poor boys. Give them books free. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Keep Twelve Tissue Remedies or some household remedies and treat the poor. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">If anyone is suffering from acute pain, shampoo the painful part. Feel you are shampooing the body of the Lord. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Do not make any difference between menial and respectable work. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Keep always some small coins in your pocket and distribute them to the poor and the decrepit. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Feed the poor. Clothe the naked. Comfort the distressed. Remove glass pieces from the road. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">There are three kinds of Karma, viz., Sanchita, Prarabdha and Agami or Kriyamana. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Sanchita is the accumulated storehouse of actions of previous births. Prarabdha is that part of Karma which has given rise to your present birth. Agami is current action. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Sanchita is destroyed by Brahma-Jnana. You will have to enjoy the Prarabdha. &nbsp;Agami has no binding force as there is no agency or egoism in the sage. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Do not be attached to the work itself. You must be able to give it up at any moment. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">As you sow, so you reap. Virtue gives you happiness. Vice gives you pain. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">You are the master of your destiny. You sow an action, reap a habit. You sow a habit, reap a character; you sow your character and reap a destiny. Destiny is your own making. Abandon desires and change your mode of thinking. You can conquer destiny. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Think you are man; man will you become. Think you are Brahman; Brahman will you become. This is the immutable divine law. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">If there is no agency, if there is no selfish motive, action becomes an inaction. You are not bound by an action. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Sastras and saints and your own pure, clean conscience will point out to you what is right, what is wrong. Follow them and do the right. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">An egoistic man alone thinks: I am the doer. Really it is the Guna or Prakriti or the sense that does the action. Atman is actionless, Akarta, Nishkriya. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Practise your Svadhanna, your Varnashrama Dharma unselfishly, without egoism. You will attain purification of heart. Knowledge of Brahman will dawn in your heart. </span></li>
</ol>
<p align="center" style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>THUS ENDS KARMA YOGA</b> <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; tab-stops: 115.5pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b>Excerpts from: </b></span><b>Karma Yoga &nbsp;- </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/amrita.htm#_VPID_3"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Amrita Gita</b></span></a></span></span><b><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
